    function setAttributeOnload(object, attribute, val) {
      if(window.addEventListener) {
        window.addEventListener('load',
          function(){ object[attribute] = val; }, false);
      } else {
        window.attachEvent('onload', function(){ object[attribute] = val; });
      }
    }
  </script>

          <div class="date-outer">
        
<h2 class='date-header'><span>Sunday, July 28, 2013</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='6622236104533634711' itemprop='blogId'/>

<a name='4500426719312677823'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
New Michael J. Fox show highlights humor in Parkinson&#39;s fight
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-4500426719312677823' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div xmlns='http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml'>Actor Michael J. Fox said he aimed to bring laughs and a dose of reality about day-to-day living with Parkinson's disease to a new NBC comedy loosely based on his life, his first lead role in a television show in 13 years.<br/><br />http://bangordailynews.com/2013/07/28/living/new-michael-j-fox-show-highlights-humor-in-parkinsons-fight/</div>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>
